# Test Cases for Cache Simulator:

## Test Case: 

### Configuration:

```
256
32
1
FIFO
WB
```

### Access sequences:
```
R: 0x1234
W: 0x5678
R: 0x1234
```

### Output:

```
Address: 0x00001234, Set: 0x1, Miss, Tag: 0x000012
Address: 0x00005678, Set: 0x3, Miss, Tag: 0x000056
Address: 0x00001234, Set: 0x1, Hit, Tag: 0x000012
```
